		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#x201C;Fiscal year 2022 was a challenging year dominated by inflation, geopolitical tensions, currency headwinds, and continuing disruptions caused by the COVID-19 pandemic</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">,&#x201D; said Steve Brass, WD-40 Company&#x2019;s president and chief executive officer. &#x201C;We learned to expect the unexpected this fiscal year and are a better prepared and more agile organization because of the challenges we&#x2019;ve faced.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">We are pleased we were able to achieve solid topline growth of our maintenance products in this volatile environment</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> including 8 percent growth of WD-40 Multi-Use Product and 19 percent growth of WD-40 Specialist</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#x201C;Unfortunately, gross margin was the Achilles heel of fiscal year 2022. </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">T</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">he current inflationary environment</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> has </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">severely disrupted our ability to achieve our 55 percent gross margin target</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> over the near-term</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">. &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">However,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> we are </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">beginning to </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">see </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">evidence</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">that</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> the gross margin restoration plan we put into place earlier this fiscal year</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> is working</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">While it might take some time, we are committed to taking the necessary actions to restore our gross margin to 55 percent over the long-term.&nbsp; </font><br /><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"></font>
		</p>

			<p style="line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt 6pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Net sales in EMEA decreased 3 percent in the fourth quarter primarily due to </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">changes in foreign currency exchange rates</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">. &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Changes in foreign currency exchange rates had an unfavorable impact on sales for the EMEA segment from period to period. On a constant currency basis, sales for the fourth quarter would have increased by 10 percent compared to the prior year fiscal quarter</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;background-color: #FFFFFF;color:#000000;"> primarily due to higher sales of WD-40 Multi-Use Product and WD-40 Specialist within certain of EMEA&#x2019;s direct and distributor markets.&nbsp;&nbsp;Also negatively impacting our net sales in the fourth quarter were</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> lower sales of homecare and cleaning products compared to the prior year period.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> The COVID-19 pandemic resulted in strong demand for homecare and cleaning products in the fourth quarter of fiscal year 2021 which was not repeated during the current year fiscal quarter.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">
			<p style="line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt 6pt;">
				<font style="margin:0.1pt 0pt 6pt;font-family:Symbol;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt 6pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Net sales in Asia-Pacific increased 18 percent in the fourth quarter primarily due to a 64 percent increase in sales in the Asia distributor markets </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">which were</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> partially offset by a 21 percent decline in sales in China. Sales of WD-40 Multi-Use Product in the Asia distributor markets, increased 66 percent </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">compared to the prior year fiscal quarter</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> Severe lockdown measures linked to the COVID-19 pandemic were lifted on June</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> 1, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">2022,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> which resulted in strong sales in the Asia distributor markets in the fourth quarter. </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Changes in foreign currency exchange rates had an unfavorable impact on sales for the Asia-Pacific segment from period to period. On a constant currency basis</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> Asia-Pacific sales for the fourth quarter would have increased by 22 percent, compared to the prior year fiscal period</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<p style="margin:0.1pt 0pt 0.1pt 36pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

		</p>

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">About WD-40 Company</font>

		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">WD-40 Company is a global marketing organization dedicated to creating positive lasting memories by developing and selling products that solve problems in workshops, factories, and homes around the world. The Company owns a wide range of well-known brands that include maintenance products and homecare and cleaning products: WD-40</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> Multi-Use Product, WD-40 Specialist</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, 3-IN-ONE</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, GT85</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, 2000 Flushes</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, no vac</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, 1001</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, Spot Shot</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, Lava</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, Solvol</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, X-14</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, and Carpet Fresh</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.</font>

<tr><td><div class="body" style="padding: 2px;">
<a href="javascript:void(0);" onclick="Show.toggleNext( this );">- Definition</a><div><p>Boolean flag that is true when the Form 8-K filing is intended to satisfy the filing obligation of the registrant as written communications pursuant to Rule 425 under the Securities Act.</p></div>
